<s> act ii scene i it is half past three <\s>

<s> act ii scene i it is half past three <\s>

<s> act ii scene i it is half past three <\s>
<s> in the kitchen of roberts's cottage a meagre little fire is burning <\s>

<s> act ii scene i it is half past three <\s>
<s> in the kitchen of roberts's cottage a meagre little fire is burning <\s>

<s> act ii scene i it is half past three <\s>

<s> act ii scene i it is half past three <\s>

<s> act ii scene i it is half past three <\s>
<s> in the kitchen of roberts's cottage a meagre little fire is burning <\s>

<s> act ii scene i it is half past three <\s>
<s> in the kitchen of roberts's cottage a meagre little fire is burning <\s>
